
CREATE TABLE tFakulteler (
    ID smallserial PRIMARY KEY,
    Adi varchar(250) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    Kisaltma varchar(10),
    Tur smallint,
    Durum boolean
);

CREATE TABLE tBolumler (
    ID smallserial PRIMARY KEY,
    Fakulte_tFakultelerID smallint REFERENCES tFakulteler(ID),
    Kisaltma varchar(30),
    Adi varchar(250)
);

CREATE TABLE tIller (
    ID smallserial PRIMARY KEY,
    Adi varchar(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE tIlceler (
    ID smallserial PRIMARY KEY,
    Adi varchar(150),
    Il_tIllerID smallint REFERENCES tIller(ID)
);

CREATE TABLE tKanGruplari (
    ID smallserial PRIMARY KEY,
    Adi char(10) UNIQUE NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE tKullanicilar (
    ID serial PRIMARY KEY,
    Adi varchar(255),
    Soyadi varchar(255),
    Eposta varchar(255) UNIQUE,
    CepTel varchar(20) UNIQUE,
    DogumTarihi date,
    DogumYeri_tIlcelerID smallint REFERENCES tIlceler(ID),
    Cinsiyet boolean,
    TCKimlikNo varchar(11) UNIQUE,
    KanGrubu_tKanGruplariID smallint REFERENCES tKanGruplari(ID)
);

CREATE TABLE tOgrenciler (
    ID serial PRIMARY KEY,
    Bolum_tBolumlerID smallint REFERENCES tBolumler(ID),
    Ogrenci_tKullanicilarID int REFERENCES tKullanicilar(ID),
    OgrenciNo varchar(9) NOT NULL,
    BaslangicTarihi date,
    MezuniyetTarihi date
);

CREATE TABLE tDersler (
    ID serial PRIMARY KEY,
    Bolum_tBolumlerID smallint REFERENCES tBolumler(ID),
    Adi varchar(250),
    Teori smallint NOT NULL,
    Uygulama smallint NOT NULL,
    AKTS smallint NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE tDersiAlanOgrenciler (
    ID serial PRIMARY KEY,
    Ders_tDerslerID int REFERENCES tDersler(ID),
    Ogrenci_tKullanicilarID int REFERENCES tKullanicilar(ID),
    Vize float,
    Final float,
    Harf varchar(5)
);

CREATE TABLE tYazOkuluUcretleri (
    ID serial PRIMARY KEY,
    Ders_tDerslerID int REFERENCES tDersler(ID),
    Ogrenci_tKullanicilarID int REFERENCES tKullanicilar(ID),
    Ucret float NOT NULL,
    IslemTarihi timestamp DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
